<h1 class="text-center">Python Video Courses</h1>
<p class="text-center text-muted">Gain practical, real-world Python skills with our library of Python video courses.</p>
<hr>
<p>Our tutorials are created, curated, and vetted by a community of expert Pythonistas. At Real Python you'll get the trusted resources you need on your path to Python mastery.</p>
<p>With new content published weekly, you'll always find something new to boost your programming skills.</p>
<p>You can mark individual lessons as completed or in-progress and learn at your own comfortable pace. Bookmark interesting lessons and review them later for optimum long-term retention.</p>
<p><strong>Not sure where to start?</strong> <a href="/onboarding-course">Check out our "Welcome to Real Python" onboarding course</a> where you’ll get an overview of the features of the Real Python platform.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="card-body d-flex flex-column">
<h2 class="card-title mt-0 "><a class="link-unstyled" href="/courses/intro-sorting-algorithms/">Introduction to Sorting Algorithms in Python</a></h2>
<div class="container">
<div class="row">
<div class="col-2 col-md-1 p-0 align-self-center">
<a href="/courses/intro-sorting-algorithms/#team"><img loading="lazy" src="https://robocrop.realpython.net/?url=https%3A//files.realpython.com/media/headshot.51ed82829b7e.jpeg&amp;w=400&amp;h=400&amp;mode=crop&amp;sig=89ffd88bf2c515c5a173c4009300f3e1fa522490" srcset="https://robocrop.realpython.net/?url=https%3A//files.realpython.com/media/headshot.51ed82829b7e.jpeg&amp;w=100&amp;h=100&amp;mode=crop&amp;sig=baf54e28b75316ed4f0a9ba3743a72ca197521fa 100w, https://robocrop.realpython.net/?url=https%3A//files.realpython.com/media/headshot.51ed82829b7e.jpeg&amp;w=200&amp;h=200&amp;mode=crop&amp;sig=6dedebc03e6ec8aa75b654101f0ade535e9c3bcf 200w, https://robocrop.realpython.net/?url=https%3A//files.realpython.com/media/headshot.51ed82829b7e.jpeg&amp;w=400&amp;h=400&amp;mode=crop&amp;sig=89ffd88bf2c515c5a173c4009300f3e1fa522490 400w" sizes="10vw" class="rounded-circle img-fluid w-100" alt="Liam Pulsifer"></a>

<p class="card-text text-muted mt-3">In this course, you&#x27;ll learn all about five different sorting algorithms in Python from both a theoretical and a practical standpoint. You&#x27;ll also learn several related and important concepts, including Big O notation and recursion.</p>

<h2 class="card-title mt-0 "><a class="link-unstyled" href="/courses/django-rest-framework/">Building With Django REST Framework</a></h2>
<div class="container">
<div class="row">
<div class="col-2 col-md-1 p-0 align-self-center">

<p class="card-text text-muted mt-3">This course will get you ready to build with Django REST Framework. The Django REST framework (DRF) is a toolkit built on top of the Django web framework that reduces the amount of code you need to write to create REST interfaces.</p>

Knowing how to handle these exceptions is essential to writing good Python code.</p>

<div class="container">

<h2 class="card-title mt-0 "><a class="link-unstyled" href="/courses/python-decorators-101/">Python Decorators 101</a></h2>

</div>
<div class="col pr-0 d-flex align-items-center">
<p class="my-0">
<span class="text-muted">
<span class="mr-2"><a class="text-muted" href="/courses/python-decorators-101/#team">Christopher Bailey</a></span>
<span class="mr-2">20 Lessons</span>

<a href="/tutorials/intermediate/" target="_blank" class="badge badge-light text-muted">intermediate</a>

</span>
</p>
 </div>
</div>
</div>
<p class="card-text text-muted mt-3">In this course on Python decorators, you&#x27;ll learn what they are and how to create and use them. Decorators provide a simple syntax for calling higher-order functions in Python. By definition, a decorator is a function that takes another function and extends the behavior of the latter function without explicitly modifying it.</p>

<p class="card-text text-muted mt-3">The &quot;requests&quot; library is the de facto standard for making HTTP requests in Python. It abstracts the complexities of making requests behind a beautiful, simple API so that you can focus on interacting with services and consuming data in your application. This course shows you how to work effectively with &quot;requests&quot;, from start to finish.</p>

<h2 class="card-title mt-0 "><a class="link-unstyled" href="/courses/staticmethod-vs-classmethod-python/">@staticmethod vs @classmethod in Python</a></h2>
<div class="container">
<div class="row">

<h2 class="card-title mt-0 "><a class="link-unstyled" href="/courses/python-for-loop/">For Loops in Python (Definite Iteration)</a></h2>

<script>
      (function(document, history, location) {
        var HISTORY_SUPPORT = !!(history && history.pushState);

        var anchorScrolls = {
          ANCHOR_REGEX: /^#[^ ]+$/,
          OFFSET_HEIGHT_PX: 120,

          /**
           * Establish events, and fix initial scroll position if a hash is provided.
           */
          init: function() {
            this.scrollToCurrent();
            window.addEventListener('hashchange', this.scrollToCurrent.bind(this));
            document.body.addEventListener('click', this.delegateAnchors.bind(this));
          },

          /**
           * Return the offset amount to deduct from the normal scroll position.
           * Modify as appropriate to allow for dynamic calculations
           */
          getFixedOffset: function() {
            return this.OFFSET_HEIGHT_PX;
          },

          /**
           * If the provided href is an anchor which resolves to an element on the
           * page, scroll to it.
           * @param  {String} href
           * @return {Boolean} - Was the href an anchor.
           */
          scrollIfAnchor: function(href, pushToHistory) {
            var match, rect, anchorOffset;

            if(!this.ANCHOR_REGEX.test(href)) {
              return false;
            }

            match = document.getElementById(href.slice(1));

            if(match) {
              rect = match.getBoundingClientRect();
              anchorOffset = window.pageYOffset + rect.top - this.getFixedOffset();
              window.scrollTo(window.pageXOffset, anchorOffset);

              // Add the state to history as-per normal anchor links
              if(HISTORY_SUPPORT && pushToHistory) {
                history.pushState({}, document.title, location.pathname + href);
              }
            }

            return !!match;
          },

          /**
           * Attempt to scroll to the current location's hash.
           */
          scrollToCurrent: function() {
            this.scrollIfAnchor(window.location.hash);
          },

          /**
           * If the click event's target was an anchor, fix the scroll position.
           */
          delegateAnchors: function(e) {
            var elem = e.target;

            if(
              elem.nodeName === 'A' &&
              this.scrollIfAnchor(elem.getAttribute('href'), true)
            ) {
              e.preventDefault();
            }
          }
        };

        window.addEventListener(
          'DOMContentLoaded', anchorScrolls.init.bind(anchorScrolls)
        );
      })(window.document, window.history, window.location);
    </script>

          e.preventDefault();
          e.currentTarget.parentElement.submit();
        })

    })();
